  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=8.5)
    The abandoned spaceport customs office creates a powerful liminal space that mirrors Vera's emotional state—forgotten yet still functioning. Sensory details like the "eternal hum of server rooms" and the decay smell of the chest establish atmosphere effectively. The setting works exceptionally well as both physical location and metaphorical space where past and present, tradition and innovation intersect. The sci-fi elements blend seamlessly with emotional storytelling.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=9.2)

The atmosphere maintains perfect tonal consistency, with the clinical detachment of Marcus's observations contrasting effectively with the supernatural implications.
